languages and frameworks (correct)\n- All languages and frameworks (incorrect)\n\nUse dashes for unordered lists.\n\nBold keywords at list start and follow with a colon.\n\n### Images\n\nInclude user.UIDToIDHandler(userService)\n   601→\n   602→\treturn func(c *contextmodel.ReqContext) {\n   603→\t\tuserID := web.Params(c.Req)[paramName]\n   604→\t\tid, err := handler(c.Req.Context(), userID)\n   605→\t\tif err == nil {\n   606→\t\t\tgotParams := web.Params(c.Req)\n   607→\t\t\tgotParams[paramName] = id\n   608→\t\t\tweb.SetURLParams(c.Req, gotParams)\n   609→\t\t} else {\n   610→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, user.ErrUserNotFound) {\n   611→\t\t\t\tc.JsonApiErr(http.StatusNotFound, \"User not found\", nil)\n   612→\t\t\t} else {\n   613→\t\t\t\tc.JsonApiErr(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"Failed to resolve user\", err)\n   614→\t\t\t}\n   615→\t\t}\n   616→\t}\n   617→}\n   618→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
